(By Order)

Public Notice U/s 485 of the Companies Act, 1956
Notice is hereby given that pursuant to the provisions of the Section 494(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956, the
members of M/s United Bright Metals Private Limited (“The Company”) at the extraordinary general meeting of the members
held on 8th day of March 2017 at 10.30 a.m. At No.94, Dr. Nanjappa Road, Coimbatore - 641 018, Tamil Nadu, passed the
following special resolution:
Member’s Voluntary Winding up under Section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956.
“RESOLVED THAT pursuant to the provisions of Section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956 (hereinafter called
“Act”) and other applicable provisions of the Act, if any, and / or The Companies Act, 2013 (including any amendment
or re-enactment thereof) and in accordance with the provisions of the Articles of Association of the Company, the consent
of the members of the Company be and is hereby accorded to wind up the affairs of the Company as member’s
voluntary winding up, with effect from the date of passing of this resolution.”
“RESOLVED FURTHER THAT pursuant to the provisions of Sections 484 to 498 of the Companies Act, 1956 and
all other applicable statutes, the company hereby resolves to carry out the complete voluntary liquidation by way of
distribution of surplus assets in cash.”
“RESOLVED FURTHER THAT pursuant to the provisions of Section 486 of Companies Act, 1956 upon the
passing of this Special Resolution a voluntary winding up shall be deemed to commence.”

684

TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE

[Part VI—Sec. 4

“RESOLVED FURTHER THAT pursuant to the provisions of Section 490 of the Companies Act, 1956,
M/s. S. Karunamoorthy, Advocates, High Court Madras, having office at No.250, Poonamallee High Road, Aminjikarai,
Chennai-600 029, be and is hereby appointed as “the Liquidator of the Company” for the purpose of the member’s voluntary
winding up to wind up the affairs of the Company at a remuneration of Rs. 4,00,000I- (Rupees Four Lakhs only) net of
service tax and other Taxes and cesses and reimbursement of actual out of pocket expenses for the winding up of the affairs
of the Company.”
“RESOLVED FURTHER THAT M/s. S. Karunamoorthy, Advocates, the Liquidator be and is hereby authorised to
exercise all the powers under Section 512 of the Companies Act, 1956 as may be applicable, to effectively wind up
the affairs of the Company.”
“RESOLVED FURTHER THAT pursuant to the provisions of Section 491 of Companies Act, 1956 and upon the
passing of this Special Resolution, the power of the Board of Directors of the Company shall cease except notice of
appointment under section 493 of the Act, which powers the Liquidator shall then assume, for the purpose of carrying out
his duties and functions as a Liquidator, in order to effect the liquidation of the company, and for all matters
incidental and consequential thereto.”
“RESOLVED FURTHER THAT the Liquidator be and is hereby authorised to exercise all or any of the power given
to him, expressly or implied, under the Companies Act, 1956 and/or Companies Act, 2013 as may be applicable to
effectively wind up the affairs of the Company.”
“RESOLVED FURTHER THAT notwithstanding the appointment of Liquidator, the board of directors of the

Pursuant to section 485 of the Companies Act 1956, notice is hereby given that in an Extraordinary General
Meeting of the members of the Company held on Thursday the 16-03-2017 at 10 A.M. at the Registered Office of the
Company the following Special Resolution was passed by the members to voluntarily wind up M/s Nimeshika Software
Consultancy and Management Private Limted.
“RESOLVED THAT pursuant to the provisions of section 484(1)(b) of the Companies Act, 1956, as may be
applicable, and other applicable provisions, if any, of the Companies Act, 1956, Companies Act, 2013 (including any
amendment or re-enactment thereof), Rules made there under and in accordance with the provisions of the Articles of
Association of the Company the consent of the members of the Company be and is hereby accorded to wind up the affairs
of the Company as the members’ voluntary winding up, with effect from the date of passing of this resolution.”
“RESOLVED FURTHER THAT upon the taking effect of relevant provisions of the Insolvency and Bankruptcy
Code 2016, with respect to the Voluntary Winding up of the Company, references to any provisions of the Companies Act,
1956 and / or Companies Act, 2013 would deemed to be in references to the Corresponding Provisions of Insolvency
and Bankruptcy Code, 2016 and the rules made there under.
